[30;1m117 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m118 | [0m[35mThe motivation for `httpcore` is:[0m
[30;1m119 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m120 | [0m[35m* To provide a reusable low-level client library, that other packages can then build on top of.[0m
[30;1m121 | [0m[35m* To provide a *really clear interface split* between the networking code and client logic,[0m
[30;1m122 | [0m[35m  so that each is easier to understand and reason about in isolation.[0m
[30;1m123 | [0m[35m[0m
